TAGS: [######] 
TOKENS: [###%]
* Tags are sequential and continue from last number used.
* Tokens - Represents how full the conversation glass is compared to GPT-5â€™s stable memory capacity. Reset this with each new chat. It needs to be a clear representation of the in-chats token amount so I can tell when its nearing capacity
	* **0%** = empty glass (new chat, no weight).
	* **100%** = full glass (at limit, must start a new chat to avoid overflow).
	* **%** should steadily climb with each scene as content builds.
